  <script>
   function getCookie(name, defaultValue) {
		match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(name + '=([^;]+)'));

		return match ? match[1] : defaultValue;
	}

	// Dynamic script loader with optional callback.
	(function(baseObj) {
		baseObj.scriptReady = function(src, attributes, callback) {
			var s = document.querySelector('script[src="' + src + '"]');

			if (s === null) {
				// Create the script tag.
				var h = document.querySelector('head');
				s = document.createElement('script');
				s.src = src;
				s.type='text/javascript';

				// Add optional attributes.
				if (typeof attributes == 'object') {
					for (var name in attributes) {
						if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(attributes, name)) {
							s.setAttribute(name, attributes[name]);
						}
					}
				}

				h.appendChild(s);

				// Add eventlistener for the callback
				if (typeof callback == 'function') {
					s.addEventListener('load', callback);
				}
			} else {
				if (typeof callback == 'function') {
					setTimeout(callback, 1);
				}
			}
		}
	})(window);
  </script>

	function capitalizeFirstLetter(string) {
		return string.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + string.slice(1);
	}
	
	function camelize(str) {
		return str.replace(/(?:^\w|[A-Z]|\b\w|\s+)/g, function(match, index) {
		if (+match === 0) return ""; // or if (/\s+/.test(match)) for white spaces
			return index === 0 ? match.toLowerCase() : match.toUpperCase();
		});
	}
	
	function replaceSpecificChars(string) {
		/*
			For replacing a single time:
			string.replace("_", " ").replace("-", " ");
			For replacing multiple times:
			string.replace(/_/g, " ").replace(/-/g, " ");
		*/
		return string.replace(/_/g, " ").replace(/-/g, " ");
	}

	function isSpecificCustomerGroup(currentCustomerGroup, array, currentValue) {
		var returnValue = false;

		for (j = 0; j < array.length; j++) {
			if (currentCustomerGroup === array[j]) {
				returnValue = true;
				break;
			} else {
				returnValue = currentValue;
			}
		}
		return returnValue;
	}

	var uData = getCookie('_uData', 'false');
	var loggedIn = 'false';

	if (uData !== 'false') {
		uData = uData.replace(/\"/g, ''); // remove quotes in the string
		loggedIn = 'true';
		var isEpaper = false;
		var isPrint = false;
		var customerGroups = JSON.parse(atob(uData)).crm_customergroups;

		if (customerGroups) {
			var customerGroupsArray = customerGroups.split(',');
			var isEpaperAddonEntitled = false;
			var isEpaperBasic = false;
			var isPrint = false;
			var isPrintAddonEntitled = false;
			var isPrintBasic = false;

			for (var i = 0; i < customerGroupsArray.length; i++) {
				// Trim the excess whitespace.
				var customerGroup = customerGroupsArray[i].replace(/^\s*/, "").replace(/\s*$/, "");
				tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userCustomerGroup" + capitalizeFirstLetter(camelize(replaceSpecificChars(customerGroup))), "true"]);
				if (customerGroup.includes("a-epaper")) {
					isEpaper = true;
				}
				isEpaperAddonEntitled = isSpecificCustomerGroup(customerGroup, ["a-epaper", "a-epaper-addon"], isEpaperAddonEntitled);
				isEpaperBasic = isSpecificCustomerGroup(customerGroup, ["a-epaper-short", "a-epaper-short-neg", "a-epaper-trial", "a-epaper-zisch", "a-epaper-discount", "a-epaper-students", "a-epaper-staff", "a-epaper-free"], isEpaperBasic);
				if (customerGroup.includes("a-print")) {
					isPrint = true;
				}
				isPrintAddonEntitled = isSpecificCustomerGroup(customerGroup, ["a-print", "a-print-partial-weekend"], isPrintAddonEntitled);
				isPrintBasic = isSpecificCustomerGroup(customerGroup, ["a-print-short", "a-print-partial", "a-print-trial", "a-print-students", "a-print-staff", "a-print-free", "a-print-discount", "a-print-zisch", "a-print-audio"], isPrintBasic);
			}
			
			if (isEpaperAddonEntitled) {
				tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userCustomerGroupAEpaperAddonEntitled", "true"]);
			}
			if (isEpaperBasic) {
				tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userCustomerGroupAEpaperBasic", "true"]);
			}
			
			if (isPrintAddonEntitled) {
				tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userCustomerGroupAPrintAddonEntitled", "true"]);
			}
			if (isPrintBasic) {
				tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userCustomerGroupAPrintBasic", "true"]);
			}

		}
		
		tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userCustomerGroupAEpaperAny", isEpaper.toString()]);
		tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userCustomerGroupAPrintAny", isPrint.toString()]);
		
		var newsletterSubscriptionsObject = JSON.parse(atob(uData)).crm_nl_optins;
		tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userHasNewsletter", (newsletterSubscriptionsObject != "").toString()]);
		if (newsletterSubscriptionsObject) {
			for (key in newsletterSubscriptionsObject) {
				var hasNewsletter = "false";
				if (newsletterSubscriptionsObject[key] === 1) {
					hasNewsletter = "true";
				}
				tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userNewsletter" + capitalizeFirstLetter(camelize(replaceSpecificChars(key.replace("a_nl_", "")))), hasNewsletter]);
			}
		}
	}
	
	tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userLoginState", loggedIn]);
	
	var gd = getCookie('_gd', 'false');
	var hasGrant = 'false';
	var hasZuckergussGrant = 'false';
	if (gd !== 'false') {
		gd = gd.replace(/\"/g, '');
		hasGrant = gd.split(',')[1];
		hasZuckergussGrant = gd.split(',')[2];
	}

	tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userGrantPremium", hasGrant]);
	tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userGrantZuckerguss", hasZuckergussGrant]);
	
	tp.push(["addHandler", "checkoutCustomEvent", function(pianoEvent) {
		console.log(pianoEvent);
		switch(pianoEvent.eventName) {
			case "external-tracking":
				wtsPianoDelayed.push(
					pianoEvent.params.href,
					['send', 'click',{ linkId:pianoEvent.params.webtrekklinkid }],
					pianoEvent.params.target
				);
				break;
			case "bus-call":
				if (window.wts) {
					wts.push([
						'send',
						'click',
						{linkId: pianoEvent.params.webtrekklinkid}]
					);
				}

				AA.bus.publish(pianoEvent.params.busAction, {webtrekkId: pianoEvent.params.webtrekklinkid});
				break;
		}
	}]);
	
	window.wtsPianoDelayed = {
		push: function(href, data, target) {
			window.setTimeout(function() {
				if (target == '_blank') {
					window.open(href,'_blank');
				} else {
					window.location.href = href;
				}
			}, 300);

			if (window.wts) {
				wts.push(data);
			}
		}
	};

	function cx_hasLocalStorage() {
		try {
			return (typeof window.localStorage === 'object') && (typeof window.localStorage.getItem === 'function');
		} catch (e) {
			return false;
		}
	}

	function cx_getOptOutStatus(key) {
		var status = false;

		if (cx_hasLocalStorage()) {
			var optedOut = window.localStorage.getItem(key);

			if (optedOut && optedOut === 'true') {
				status = true;
			}
		}

		return status;
	}

	function pianoInitWithConsent() {
		if (uData !== 'false') {
			uData = uData.replace(/\"/g, ''); // remove quotes in the string
			tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userId", JSON.parse(atob(uData)).sso_user_id]);
		}

		var cxOptOut = cx_getOptOutStatus('cx_optOut');
		console.log('cx_optOut: ' + cxOptOut);

		cX = window.cX || { options: { consent: cxOptOut } }
		cX.callQueue = cX.callQueue || [];

		(function (waitTimeout) {
			var p = new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
				var dmpSegments = {
					segmentIds: [],
					updated: false
				};
				var segmentFetchSuccess = false
				cX.callQueue.push(['invoke', function () {
					try {
						cX.getUserSegmentIds({
							persistedQueryId: 'f53a8bf3267eeb6c4bdd07b68c73c658042d3c72', 
							callback: function (segments) { 
								if (segments && segments.length > 0) { 
									dmpSegments.segmentIds = segments; 
									for (var j = 0; j < segments.length; j++) { 
										tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userDmpSegmentId"+segments[j], "true"]); 
									} 
								}
								tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userDmpUserId", cX.getUserId()]);
								tp.push(["setCustomVariable", "userDmpSiteId", "1138571157941481569"]);
								segmentFetchSuccess = true; resolve() 
							} 
						}); 
					} 
					catch (e) { reject() } 
					setTimeout(
						function () { 
							if (!segmentFetchSuccess) { reject() } 
						}, 
						waitTimeout
					) 
				}]); 
			}) 
			p.then(
				function () { 
					console.log('Segments fetched successfully'); 
					tp.push(["init", function () { tp.experience.init(); }]); 
				}, 
				function () {

					tp.push(["init", function () { tp.experience.init(); }]); 
				}
			)
		})(1000);
	}

   function getNewsletterSubscriptions(key) {
		var newsletterSubscriptions = '';
		if (uData !== 'false') {
			var newsletterSubscriptionsObject = JSON.parse(atob(uData))[key];
			if (newsletterSubscriptionsObject) {
				for (key in newsletterSubscriptionsObject) {
					if (newsletterSubscriptionsObject[key] === 1) {
						if (newsletterSubscriptions !== '') {
							newsletterSubscriptions += ','
						}
						newsletterSubscriptions += key;
					}
				}
			}
		}
		return newsletterSubscriptions;
	}

	function modifyUrl(url) {
		const onlyParams = window.location.search;
		const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(onlyParams);
		var urlParamsToRemove = ["fbclid", "gclid"];
		for (i = 0; i < urlParamsToRemove.length; i++) {
			var urlParam = urlParamsToRemove[i];
			var urlParamString = "&"+urlParam;
			if(urlParams.has(urlParam)) {
				if(onlyParams.includes("?"+urlParam)) {
					urlParamString = "?"+urlParam;
				}
				url = url.replace(urlParamString+"="+urlParams.get(urlParam), "");
			}
		}
		return url;
	}

       <section class="p-block p-marg_v-xl">
        <div class="p-grid p-grid--1-1 p-grid--wrap">
         <a class="p-swatch_topdown-nice p-blocklink" data-action-tracking="ressort-pro-kontra-startseite-desktop-1" href="https://www.augsburger-allgemeine.de/kultur/Journal/Die-Spuelmaschine-umraeumen-Na-klar-id59341431.html" title="Die Spülmaschine umräumen? Na klar!">
          <div class="p-pos_rel">
           <picture class="b-picture p-dsply_blck q-media-format--half" data-behaviour="lazy">
            <img alt="Unordentliche Spülmaschinen sind ein Albtraum, findet unsere Autorin." data-lazy-src="https://www.augsburger-allgemeine.de/img/bilder/crop59341981/9526997241-cv16_9-w460/Copy-of-Spuelmaschine-pro.jpg" data-lazy-srcset="https://www.augsburger-allgemeine.de/img/bilder/crop59341981/9526997241-cv16_9-w460/Copy-of-Spuelmaschine-pro.jpg 460w, https://www.augsburger-allgemeine.de/img/bilder/crop59341981/638018770-cv16_9-w920/Copy-of-Spuelmaschine-pro.jpg 920w" sizes="460px" src="https://www.augsburger-allgemeine.de/resources/38257-1/ver1-0/img/placeholder/16x9.png" title=""/>

           Pro-Kommentar
          </span>
          <h3 class="p-fnt_cnd-bold--l p-fnt_letter-spacing--zero p-line-clamp_two p-marg_t-l p-marg_h-xl">
           Die Spülmaschine umräumen? Na klar!
          </h3>
          <p class="p-fnt_std-normal--s p-line-clamp_three p-marg_v-xl p-marg_h-xl">
           Vogelwildes Einräumen in die Spülmaschine geht gar nicht, findet unsere Autorin.
          </p>
         </a>
         <a class="p-swatch_topdown-nice p-blocklink" data-action-tracking="ressort-pro-kontra-startseite-desktop-2" href="https://www.augsburger-allgemeine.de/kultur/Journal/Die-Spuelmaschine-umraeumen-Bloss-nicht-id59341451.html" title="Die Spülmaschine umräumen? Bloß nicht!">
          <div class="p-pos_rel">
           <picture class="b-picture p-dsply_blck q-media-format--half" data-behaviour="lazy">
            <img alt="Nachsortieren ist unhöflich, meint unsere Autorin." data-lazy-src="https://www.augsburger-allgemeine.de/img/bilder/crop59341996/3256999565-cv16_9-w460/Copy-of-Spuelmaschine-contra.jpg" data-lazy-srcset="https://www.augsburger-allgemeine.de/img/bilder/crop59341996/3256999565-cv16_9-w460/Copy-of-Spuelmaschine-contra.jpg 460w, https://www.augsburger-allgemeine.de/img/bilder/crop59341996/1680183094-cv16_9-w920/Copy-of-Spuelmaschine-contra.jpg 920w" sizes="460px" src="https://www.augsburger-allgemeine.de/resources/38257-1/ver1-0/img/placeholder/16x9.png" title=""/>
           </picture>
           <div class="p-pos_abs-bot-rig p-pad_a-m">
           </div>
          </div>
          <span class="p-fnt_std-bold--xs-uc-ul p-fnt_letter-spacing--one p-line-clamp_one p-clr_sld p-marg_t-xl p-marg_h-xl">
           Kontra-Kommentar
          </span>
          <div class="p-comment-count p-icon_comment_bubble p-marg_t-xl p-marg_r-xl" data-comments-counter="1">
          </div>
          <h3 class="p-fnt_cnd-bold--l p-fnt_letter-spacing--zero p-line-clamp_two p-marg_t-l p-marg_h-xl">
           Die Spülmaschine umräumen? Bloß nicht!
          </h3>
          <p class="p-fnt_std-normal--s p-line-clamp_three p-marg_v-xl p-marg_h-xl">
           Wer zuerst einräumt, bestimmt die (Un-)Ordnung in der Spülmaschine, findet unsere Autorin.
          </p>

          Günzburg
         </span>
         <h3 class="p-fnt_cnd-bold--l p-fnt_letter-spacing--zero p-line-clamp_three p-marg_t-l p-marg_h-xl">
          Vize-Kreisvorsitzender Schwarz spricht über Dilemma der CSU im Kreis Günzburg
         </h3>
         <p class="p-fnt_std-normal--s p-line-clamp_five p-marg_v-xl p-marg_h-xl">
          <span class="aa-plus aa-plus-mini">
           Plus
          </span>
          Am Samstag hatten Parteimitglieder noch keine Gelegenheit, mit Sauter zu sprechen. Delegierte wurden gewählt, die einen noch unbekannten Kandidaten für die Bundestagswahl nominieren sollen.
         </p>
        </a>
        <a class="p-swatch_topdown-nice p-blocklink" data-action-tracking="ressort-bayern-reihe3-startseite-desktop-2" href="https://www.augsburger-allgemeine.de/bayern/Wo-gilt-die-naechtliche-Ausgangssperre-in-Bayern-am-21-Maerz-id59120436.html" title="Wo gilt die nächtliche Ausgangssperre in Bayern am 21. März?">
         <div class="p-pos_rel">
          <picture class="b-picture p-dsply_blck q-media-format--third" data-behaviour="lazy">

          Ausgangssperre in Bayern
         </span>
         <h3 class="p-fnt_cnd-bold--l p-fnt_letter-spacing--zero p-line-clamp_three p-marg_t-l p-marg_h-xl">
          Wo gilt die nächtliche Ausgangssperre in Bayern am 21. März?
         </h3>
         <p class="p-fnt_std-normal--s p-line-clamp_five p-marg_v-xl p-marg_h-xl">
          In Bayern gibt es die nächtliche Ausgangssperre nur noch in Corona-Hotspots. Diese Landkreise und Städte sind aktuell betroffen.
         </p>
        </a>
        <a class="p-swatch_topdown-nice p-blocklink" data-action-tracking="ressort-bayern-monitor-startseite-desktop-1" href="/special/bayern-monitor/" title="Wir möchten wissen, wie Bayern tickt: Stimmen Sie hier ab">
         <div class="p-pos_rel">

          Bayern-Monitor
         </span>
         <h3 class="p-fnt_cnd-bold--l p-fnt_letter-spacing--zero p-line-clamp_three p-marg_t-l p-marg_h-xl">
          Wir möchten wissen, wie Bayern tickt: Stimmen Sie hier ab
         </h3>
         <p class="p-fnt_std-normal--s p-line-clamp_five p-marg_v-xl p-marg_h-xl">
          Was bewegt die Menschen im Freistaat? Das wollen wir gemeinsam mit Ihnen herausfinden. Wie unser Bayern-Monitor funktioniert und wie Sie mitmachen können.

         <span class="p-fnt_std-bold--xs-uc-ul p-fnt_letter-spacing--one p-line-clamp_one p-clr_sld p-marg_t-xl p-marg_h-xl">
          Tatort
         </span>
         <h3 class="p-fnt_cnd-bold--l p-fnt_letter-spacing--zero p-line-clamp_three p-marg_t-l p-marg_h-xl">
          Lohnt sich das Einschalten? So wird der Kölner "Tatort" am Sonntag
         </h3>
         <p class="p-fnt_std-normal--s p-line-clamp_five p-marg_v-xl p-marg_h-xl">
          Ballauf und Schenk ermitteln im Schatten des Kölner Doms. Und dort sehen sie viel Elend. Das können sie sogar bei ihrem Stamm-Imbiss beobachten. Wieder einmal ein sozialkritischer "Tatort".
         </p>
        </a>
        <div class="p-swatch_topdown-nice p-blocklink" data-autofetch-chunk-endpoint="https://www.augsburger-allgemeine.de/widget/id50006941?ctxSec=1&amp;view=default_ajax&amp;ctxArt=59309136" data-autofetch-chunk-method="post" data-component="autofetch-chunk">
        </div>
       </div>
      </section>

          So klappt's
         </span>
         <h3 class="p-fnt_cnd-bold--l p-fnt_letter-spacing--zero p-line-clamp_three p-marg_t-l p-marg_h-xl">
          Diese zehn Tipps helfen beim Autoverkauf

         <p class="p-fnt_std-normal--s p-line-clamp_five p-marg_v-xl p-marg_h-xl">

          Arbeit im Home Office

         </span>
         <div class="p-comment-count p-icon_comment_bubble p-marg_t-xl p-marg_r-xl" data-comments-counter="1">

         <h3 class="p-fnt_cnd-bold--l p-fnt_letter-spacing--zero p-line-clamp_three p-marg_t-l p-marg_h-xl">
          Europa wird in den USA vom Vorbild zum Schreckgespenst
         </h3>
         <p class="p-fnt_std-normal--s p-line-clamp_five p-marg_v-xl p-marg_h-xl">
          Steigende Corona-Infektionszahlen, chaotische Krisenpolitik und eine stockende Impfkampagne: Das liberale Amerika blickt zunehmend befremdet über den Atlantik.
         </p>
        </a>
        <div class="p-vlist p-vlist--stretch">
         <div class="p-swatch_topdown-nice--trans-fake p-vlist p-clearfix">

         </span>
         <h3 class="p-fnt_cnd-bold--l p-fnt_letter-spacing--zero p-line-clamp_three p-marg_t-l p-marg_h-xl">

         </h3>
         <p class="p-fnt_std-normal--s p-line-clamp_five p-marg_v-xl p-marg_h-xl">

           Exklusiv
          </span>
          „In Sachen Gleichberechtigung ist Deutschland weit abgeschlagen“, sagt die frühere Siemens-Personalchefin Janina Kugel. Sie beklagt fehlende Impulse in der Gesetzgebung.
         </p>
        </a>

          Corona-Gipfel
         </span>
         <div class="p-comment-count p-icon_comment_bubble p-marg_t-xl p-marg_r-xl" data-comments-counter="4">
         </div>
         <h3 class="p-fnt_cnd-bold--l p-fnt_letter-spacing--zero p-line-clamp_three p-marg_t-l p-marg_h-xl">
          Händler warnen vor neuem Lockdown
         </h3>
         <p class="p-fnt_std-normal--s p-line-clamp_five p-marg_v-xl p-marg_h-xl">
          s.Oliver-Chef Claus-Dietrich Lahrs fordert vor dem Corona-Gipfel am Montag eine weitere Öffnung im Handel. Der Handelsverband warnt vor einem neuen Lockdown.
         </p>

         </span>
         <h3 class="p-fnt_cnd-bold--l p-fnt_letter-spacing--zero p-line-clamp_three p-marg_t-l p-marg_h-xl">
